Animatory state tiles

Click a tile in the gallery below to see the following info:

0: row 1, column 1
lsb=130, ref_page=221
ref_addr=(lsb,ref_page)=56706
ref=3, udg_page=199
udg_addr=(ref,udg_page)=50947

where:

  • lsb is the animatory state + 128 + n (n=2 if the animatory state is divisible by 8, n=0 otherwise)
  • ref_page is the page containing the UDG reference for the tile (215-229)
  • ref_addr is the address of the UDG reference (lsb+256*ref_page)
  • ref is the UDG reference at ref_addr (0-214, 217-255)
  • udg_page is the base page for the tile graphic data (always 199)
  • udg_addr is the base address of the tile graphic data (ref+256*udg_page)

The graphic for an animatory state is made up of 4 or 15 tiles in a 2x2, 3x5 or 5x3, grid:

02
13
0510
1611
2712
3813
4914
036912
1471013
2581114

Each tile has a UDG reference (ref) located at (lsb,T+215), where T is the tile number (0-14).

The eight graphic bytes and eight mask bytes for a tile are located thus:

AddressContents
(ref,udg_page)=udg_addr Graphic byte 1/8
(ref,udg_page+1)=udg_addr+256 Mask byte 1/8
(ref,udg_page+2)=udg_addr+512 Graphic byte 2/8
(ref,udg_page+3)=udg_addr+768 Mask byte 2/8
(ref,udg_page+4)=udg_addr+1024 Graphic byte 3/8
(ref,udg_page+5)=udg_addr+1280 Mask byte 3/8
(ref,udg_page+6)=udg_addr+1536 Graphic byte 4/8
(ref,udg_page+7)=udg_addr+1792 Mask byte 4/8
(ref,udg_page+8)=udg_addr+2048 Graphic byte 5/8
(ref,udg_page+9)=udg_addr+2304 Mask byte 5/8
(ref,udg_page+10)=udg_addr+2560 Graphic byte 6/8
(ref,udg_page+11)=udg_addr+2816 Mask byte 6/8
(ref,udg_page+12)=udg_addr+3072 Graphic byte 7/8
(ref,udg_page+13)=udg_addr+3328 Mask byte 7/8
(ref,udg_page+14)=udg_addr+3584 Graphic byte 8/8
(ref,udg_page+15)=udg_addr+3840 Mask byte 8/8

The 'null' UDG (ref=0) is always taken to be blank (eight zeroes); its graphic data is not looked up at (0,199).

Any given tile (identified by udg_addr) may appear in more than one animatory state (and in more than one place in a single animatory state).

The tiles for animatory states 128-255 are not stored separately; the tiles for animatory state N>=128 are obtained by flipping the tiles for animatory state N-128 (see 59635).
